codex
## Findings

1. **HIGH — Protected auth data is still logged after denial.**  
   The plan only forbids logging inside the adapter ([plan:76](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/.planning/superpowers/plans/2026-07-13-security-535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit-plan.md:76)). Every request—including a limiter-denied request—then reaches the postroute hook, which reparses and logs `req$postBody` ([mount_endpoints.R:169](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/api/bootstrap/mount_endpoints.R:169)). The sanitizer does not redact `email` or `user_name` ([logging_sanitizer.R:44](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/api/core/logging_sanitizer.R:44)). SMTP `conditionMessage(e)` logging may also contain a recipient address.  
   **Fix:** redact the entire body for these three paths before parsing/logging, in both file and DB logs; log generic SMTP failures without exception text or account identifiers. Add assertions against captured postroute/error logs.

2. **HIGH — New configuration never reaches the API container.**  
   Task 4 lists only `.env.example` and deployment docs ([plan:90](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/.planning/superpowers/plans/2026-07-13-security-535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit-plan.md:90)), but Compose uses an explicit environment map ([docker-compose.yml:178](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/docker-compose.yml:178)). Consequently, documented `AUTH_ENDPOINT_*` overrides—including trusted proxy CIDRs—would be silently absent. Behind an institutional proxy, all clients then share the proxy bucket, enabling broad auth denial with a few requests. Traefik requires aligned `forwardedHeaders.trustedIPs`, and normally appends the peer address to XFF ([official entrypoint documentation](https://doc.traefik.io/traefik/reference/install-configuration/entrypoints/)).  
   **Fix:** add all four variables to the API Compose environment, validate rendered Compose configuration, and live-test the two-proxy topology with two client IPs.

3. **HIGH — Process-local state is bypassable across API replicas.**  
   S6 explicitly describes its store as process-local and relies on a DB-backed global job cap as the cross-process backstop ([clustering-submit-throttle.R:12](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/api/functions/clustering-submit-throttle.R:12)). Auth has no equivalent backstop. This deployment supports scaled APIs, while sticky routing is only a client cookie ([docker-compose.yml:251](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/docker-compose.yml:251)); an attacker can discard it and multiply attempts by replica count.  
   **Fix:** retain the local generic limiter but add atomic shared/edge enforcement, or explicitly enforce one API replica plus a shared compensating control. Test without retaining sticky cookies across multiple replicas.

4. **MEDIUM — The plan permits one shared bucket across unrelated auth operations.**  
   A single auth store and guard with no required operation scope ([plan:76](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/.planning/superpowers/plans/2026-07-13-security-535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit-plan.md:76)) lets cheap authenticate attempts consume signup and reset capacity for everyone sharing an IP/NAT.  
   **Fix:** require a fixed server-owned scope per endpoint, with separate limits/buckets; optionally add a distinct aggregate auth budget.

5. **MEDIUM — Tests can pass without proving deployed endpoint behavior.**  
   The proposed handler tests inject a fake guard into extracted expressions ([plan:30](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/.planning/superpowers/plans/2026-07-13-security-535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit-plan.md:30)). They do not prove clean-process source order, actual adapter execution, mounted serialization, logging redaction, or 503 behavior. Running the generic test before the clustering test in one R process can also hide a missing dependency. The current masked-verb guard checks only calls containing `inherits=` ([test-unit-base-exists-get-guard.R:24](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/api/tests/testthat/test-unit-base-exists-get-guard.R:24)).  
   **Fix:** add clean-environment bootstrap tests with hostile masked `get`/`exists`, and mounted HTTP tests for all three routes covering real N+1 429, strict digits-only positive `Retry-After`, injected limiter failure 503, side-effect counters, body-only inputs, query rejection/ignoring, XFF alias spoofing, and log capture. Ensure the Playwright overlay retains the alias-stripping middleware; its label override currently drops it ([docker-compose.playwright.yml:67](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/docker-compose.playwright.yml:67)). Empty-valued Traefik request-header rules do remove headers as intended ([official headers documentation](https://doc.traefik.io/traefik/master/reference/routing-configuration/http/middlewares/headers/)).

Existing `mount_endpoint()` wiring remains intact, and the proposed integer conversion prevents direct `Retry-After` injection. Tests could not run in this read-only environment because R could not create temporary files.

Verdict: FIX-FIRST
tokens used
125,401
## Findings

1. **HIGH — Protected auth data is still logged after denial.**  
   The plan only forbids logging inside the adapter ([plan:76](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/.planning/superpowers/plans/2026-07-13-security-535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit-plan.md:76)). Every request—including a limiter-denied request—then reaches the postroute hook, which reparses and logs `req$postBody` ([mount_endpoints.R:169](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/api/bootstrap/mount_endpoints.R:169)). The sanitizer does not redact `email` or `user_name` ([logging_sanitizer.R:44](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/api/core/logging_sanitizer.R:44)). SMTP `conditionMessage(e)` logging may also contain a recipient address.  
   **Fix:** redact the entire body for these three paths before parsing/logging, in both file and DB logs; log generic SMTP failures without exception text or account identifiers. Add assertions against captured postroute/error logs.

2. **HIGH — New configuration never reaches the API container.**  
   Task 4 lists only `.env.example` and deployment docs ([plan:90](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/.planning/superpowers/plans/2026-07-13-security-535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit-plan.md:90)), but Compose uses an explicit environment map ([docker-compose.yml:178](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/docker-compose.yml:178)). Consequently, documented `AUTH_ENDPOINT_*` overrides—including trusted proxy CIDRs—would be silently absent. Behind an institutional proxy, all clients then share the proxy bucket, enabling broad auth denial with a few requests. Traefik requires aligned `forwardedHeaders.trustedIPs`, and normally appends the peer address to XFF ([official entrypoint documentation](https://doc.traefik.io/traefik/reference/install-configuration/entrypoints/)).  
   **Fix:** add all four variables to the API Compose environment, validate rendered Compose configuration, and live-test the two-proxy topology with two client IPs.

3. **HIGH — Process-local state is bypassable across API replicas.**  
   S6 explicitly describes its store as process-local and relies on a DB-backed global job cap as the cross-process backstop ([clustering-submit-throttle.R:12](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/api/functions/clustering-submit-throttle.R:12)). Auth has no equivalent backstop. This deployment supports scaled APIs, while sticky routing is only a client cookie ([docker-compose.yml:251](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/docker-compose.yml:251)); an attacker can discard it and multiply attempts by replica count.  
   **Fix:** retain the local generic limiter but add atomic shared/edge enforcement, or explicitly enforce one API replica plus a shared compensating control. Test without retaining sticky cookies across multiple replicas.

4. **MEDIUM — The plan permits one shared bucket across unrelated auth operations.**  
   A single auth store and guard with no required operation scope ([plan:76](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/.planning/superpowers/plans/2026-07-13-security-535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit-plan.md:76)) lets cheap authenticate attempts consume signup and reset capacity for everyone sharing an IP/NAT.  
   **Fix:** require a fixed server-owned scope per endpoint, with separate limits/buckets; optionally add a distinct aggregate auth budget.

5. **MEDIUM — Tests can pass without proving deployed endpoint behavior.**  
   The proposed handler tests inject a fake guard into extracted expressions ([plan:30](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/.planning/superpowers/plans/2026-07-13-security-535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit-plan.md:30)). They do not prove clean-process source order, actual adapter execution, mounted serialization, logging redaction, or 503 behavior. Running the generic test before the clustering test in one R process can also hide a missing dependency. The current masked-verb guard checks only calls containing `inherits=` ([test-unit-base-exists-get-guard.R:24](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/api/tests/testthat/test-unit-base-exists-get-guard.R:24)).  
   **Fix:** add clean-environment bootstrap tests with hostile masked `get`/`exists`, and mounted HTTP tests for all three routes covering real N+1 429, strict digits-only positive `Retry-After`, injected limiter failure 503, side-effect counters, body-only inputs, query rejection/ignoring, XFF alias spoofing, and log capture. Ensure the Playwright overlay retains the alias-stripping middleware; its label override currently drops it ([docker-compose.playwright.yml:67](/home/bernt-popp/development/sysndd/.claude/worktrees/535-auth-endpoint-rate-limit/docker-compose.playwright.yml:67)). Empty-valued Traefik request-header rules do remove headers as intended ([official headers documentation](https://doc.traefik.io/traefik/master/reference/routing-configuration/http/middlewares/headers/)).

Existing `mount_endpoint()` wiring remains intact, and the proposed integer conversion prevents direct `Retry-After` injection. Tests could not run in this read-only environment because R could not create temporary files.

Verdict: FIX-FIRST
